for v8, v9 in v5 do
    if v9.Island and v9.World then
        local v10 = string.lower(v8):gsub(" ", "-");
        local v11 = {};
        local v12 = false;
        for _, v14 in v6[v9.World].Islands do
            if v12 then
                table.insert(v11, v14.Name);
            elseif v14.Name == v9.Island then
                v12 = true;
            end;
        end;
        if #v11 == 0 then
            if v9.Island then
                v11 = {
                    v9.Island
                };
            else
                continue;
            end;
        end;
        v7[v10] = {
            Weight = 15, 
            Type = "Egg", 
            Egg = v8, 
            Areas = v11
        };
    end;
end;
for _, v16 in v7 do
    if v16.Type == "Chest" then
        for _, v18 in v16.Pool do
            if v18.Item.Type == "Pet" then
                local v19 = v4[v18.Item.Name];
                if v19 and v19.Chance ~= 0 then
                    v19.Chance = v18.Chance;
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;
return v7;

			Rarity = v30, 
			Amount = v13[v30]
		};
		table.insert(v18, {
			Chance = 5, 
			Item = {
				Task = v31, 
				Reward = 200
			}
		});
		v31 = {
			Type = "Hatch", 
			Rarity = v30, 
			Amount = v13[v30] * 10
		};
		table.insert(v20, {
			Chance = 5, 
			Item = {
				Task = v31, 
				Reward = 1800
			}
		});
	end;
end;
return {
	Hourly = v18, 
	Daily = v20
};
